by a constant deceleration in a distance of 22.5 m . Find the time taken for the particle to come to rest.</li>
</ol>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Just use the SUVAT equation that does not involve time to find the acceleration first, then use that to find the time.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">

<br>
<ol start="2">
<li>A plant pot falls from a balcony. It hits the ground after 2.24 seconds.<br>
(a) By modelling the plant pot as a particle, find the height of the balcony from the ground.</li>
</ol>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Use the SUVAT equation that does not involve final velocity to find the height.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">

<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">

<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Use the SUVAT equation that involves initial velocity, time and acceleration to find the distance. Find the acceleration first using the equation that involves initial velocity, final velocity and time.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>

Find the length of time that the displacement of the particle up the track from the point of projection is greater than 8 metres.</li>
</ol>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Again use the SUVAT equations. Find the time taken to reach 8 metres by rearranging the equation to form a quadratic equation.<br>
There will be two solutions, find the difference between them to get the time spent above 8 metres.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">

<div>The train then travels with constant velocity for a time, T , until it decelerates uniformly for 15 seconds, coming to rest at the station <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.717ex" height="1.545ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 759 683"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="42" d="M231 637Q204 637 199 638T194 649Q194 676 205 682Q206 683 335 683Q594 683 608 681Q671 671 713 636T756 544Q756 480 698 429T565 360L555 357Q619 348 660 311T702 219Q702 146 630 78T453 1Q446 0 242 0Q42 0 39 2Q35 5 35 10Q35 17 37 24Q42 43 47 45Q51 46 62 46H68Q95 46 128 49Q142 52 147 61Q150 65 219 339T288 628Q288 635 231 637ZM649 544Q649 574 634 600T585 634Q578 636 493 637Q473 637 451 637T416 636H403Q388 635 384 626Q382 622 352 506Q352 503 351 500L320 374H401Q482 374 494 376Q554 386 601 434T649 544ZM595 229Q595 273 572 302T512 336Q506 337 429 337Q311 337 310 336Q310 334 293 263T258 122L240 52Q240 48 252 48T333 46Q422 46 429 47Q491 54 543 105T595 229Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> which is 2.68 km away from <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.697ex" height="1.62ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -716 750 716"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="41" d="M208 74Q208 50 254 46Q272 46 272 35Q272 34 270 22Q267 8 264 4T251 0Q249 0 239 0T205 1T141 2Q70 2 50 0H42Q35 7 35 11Q37 38 48 46H62Q132 49 164 96Q170 102 345 401T523 704Q530 716 547 716H555H572Q578 707 578 706L606 383Q634 60 636 57Q641 46 701 46Q726 46 726 36Q726 34 723 22Q720 7 718 4T704 0Q701 0 690 0T651 1T578 2Q484 2 455 0H443Q437 6 437 9T439 27Q443 40 445 43L449 46H469Q523 49 533 63L521 213H283L249 155Q208 86 208 74ZM516 260Q516 271 504 416T490 562L463 519Q447 492 400 412L310 260L413 259Q516 259 516 260Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</div>
<div>Sketch a velocity time graph for the motion of the train and calculate the time taken to get between the two stations.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>There are three phases to the motion: acceleration, constant velocity and deceleration.</div>
</div>
</details>

<ol start="6">
<li>A particle travels in a straight line.<br>
The motion is modelled by the <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.097ex" height="1.027ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -443 485 454"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="76" d="M173 380Q173 405 154 405Q130 405 104 376T61 287Q60 286 59 284T58 281T56 279T53 278T49 278T41 278H27Q21 284 21 287Q21 294 29 316T53 368T97 419T160 441Q202 441 225 417T249 361Q249 344 246 335Q246 329 231 291T200 202T182 113Q182 86 187 69Q200 26 250 26Q287 26 319 60T369 139T398 222T409 277Q409 300 401 317T383 343T365 361T357 383Q357 405 376 424T417 443Q436 443 451 425T467 367Q467 340 455 284T418 159T347 40T241 -11Q177 -11 139 22Q102 54 102 117Q102 148 110 181T151 298Q173 362 173 380Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> - <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.817ex" height="1.441ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -626 361 637"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> diagram below.<br>

(a) Calculate the acceleration of the particle in the part of the motion from <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.965ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2194.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> to <span class="math-inline ">

</ol>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>The acceleration over that interval is the slope of the vt graph.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>The acceleration is given by the gradient of the <span class="math-inline ">

<div>(b) Calculate the displacement of the particle from its position when <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.965ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2194.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> to its position when <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.965ex" height="1.715ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -676 2194.6 758"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="37" d="M55 458Q56 460 72 567L88 674Q88 676 108 676H128V672Q128 662 143 655T195 646T364 644H485V605L417 512Q408 500 387 472T360 435T339 403T319 367T305 330T292 284T284 230T278 162T275 80Q275 66 275 52T274 28V19Q270 2 255 -10T221 -22Q210 -22 200 -19T179 0T168 40Q168 198 265 368Q285 400 349 489L395 552H302Q128 552 119 546Q113 543 108 522T98 479L95 458V455H55V458Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>There are three sections above the time axis and one section below it. To calculate displacement, calculate the area of each section and add them up, then subtract the area below the time axis.</div>
</div>
</details>

(a) the time for which ball A has been in motion when the balls meet</li>
</ol>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Let the time after ball A is thrown when they meet be <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.817ex" height="1.441ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -626 361 637"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> seconds. <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.817ex" height="1.441ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -626 361 637"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> need to be greater than 3 seconds since ball B is thrown 3 seconds later.</div>
<div>The displacements of ball A and ball B are same.</div>
</div>
</details>

<div>Hence ball A has been in motion for <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.131ex" height="1.532ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -677 500 677"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="34" d="M462 0Q444 3 333 3Q217 3 199 0H190V46H221Q241 46 248 46T265 48T279 53T286 61Q287 63 287 115V165H28V211L179 442Q332 674 334 675Q336 677 355 677H373L379 671V211H471V165H379V114Q379 73 379 66T385 54Q393 47 442 46H471V0H462ZM293 211V545L74 212L183 211H293Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> s when the balls meet.</div>
</div>
</details>
<br>
<div>(b) the height above P at which A and B meet.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Use either displacement equation for ball A or ball B to find the height when they meet.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">

<ol start="8">
<li>Cars A and B are traveling in the same direction along a straight road. The time <span class="math-inline ">

</ol>

<br>
<div>(b) Show that, in the first 40 seconds, car A travels 400 m further than car B.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Calculate the displacements of each car in the first 40 seconds using the area under the vt graphs.</div>
</div>
</details>

<div>Therefore the difference in the first 40 s is</div>

<div>so car A travels <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.05ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="5.844ex" height="1.581ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -677 2583 <summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>From part (b), car A catches up 400 meters at <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="6.096ex" height="1.717ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -677 2694.6 759"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="34" d="M462 0Q444 3 333 3Q217 3 199 0H190V46H221Q241 46 248 46T265 48T279 53T286 61Q287 63 287 115V165H28V211L179 442Q332 674 334 675Q336 677 355 677H373L379 671V211H471V165H379V114Q379 73 379 66T385 54Q393 47 442 46H471V0H462ZM293 211V545L74 212L183 211H293Z"></path><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z" transform="translate(500, 0)"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> s. In other words, the gap has closed from 500 m to 100 m after 40 s.<br>
After that, both cars travel at constant speeds. Find the time taken for car A to close the remaining 100 m gap.</div>

<div>so the separation closed in the first 40 s is</div>
